lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  assert |a + [x]| == |b + [y]|; // size equality
  assert |a + [x]| == |a| + 1;
  assert |b + [y]| == |b| + 1;
  assert |a| == |b|; // from requires

         DotProduct(a, b) + a[|a|] * b[|b|];
  assert a[|a|] == x;
  assert b[|b|] == y;
  // Combining the assertions gives the desired result
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert b != [];
  assert |b| == |a|;

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int

  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  // The lemma is proved by induction on |a|
  if |a| == 0 {
    // Base case: a and b are empty sequences
    assert DotProduct([], []) == 0;
    assert DotProduct([x], [y]) == x * y;
    assert 0 + x * y == x * y;
  } else {
    // Induction step
    var a' := a[..|a|-1];
    var b' := b[..|b|-1];
    var lastA := a[|a|-1];
    var lastB := b[|b|-1];
    // Apply the induction hypothesis
    assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) - lastA * lastB;
    // Now use the recursive definition of DotProduct
    assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) ==
           DotProduct(a', b') + lastA * lastB + x * y;
    assert DotProduct(a', b') + lastA * lastB == DotProduct(a, b);
    assert DotProduct(a', b') + lastA * lastB + x * y ==
           DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
  }
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      // At this point, |a[..i]| == |b| == i
      assert |a[..i]| == |b|;
      // Use the lemma to compute the new dot product after appending
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);
      // After appending, the dot product of a[..i+1] and b+[a[i+1]] satisfies:
      // DotProduct(a[..i+1], b+[a[i+1]]) == DotProduct(a[..i], b) + a[i] * a[i+1]
      // Since i is even, DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0 by the invariant
      assert DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0;
      // Therefore, the new dot product equals a[i] * a[i+1]
      // This is exactly what we need for the next iteration
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      // Here i is odd
      assert |a[..i]| == |b|;
      // Use the lemma for the negative case
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);
      // After appending, the dot product of a[..i+1] and b+[-a[i-1]] equals
      // DotProduct(a[..i], b) + a[i] * (-a[i-1])
      // By the invariant, DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i-1] * a[i]
      assert DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i];
      // So the new dot product is a[i] * (-a[i-1]) + a[i-1] * a[i]
      // which simplifies to 0
      assert a[i] * (-a[i - 1]) + a[i - 1] * a[i] == 0;
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
    decreases |a| - i
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  assert |b| == |a|;
  assert AllNonZero(b);
  assert AllBounded(b, 100);
  assert DotProduct(a, b) == 0;
}

}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);
      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);
      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
  assert ValidSolution(a, b);
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  // We prove the lemma by unfolding the definition of DotProduct.
  // Let n = |a| = |b|.
  // Then |a + [x]| = n+1 and |b + [y]| = n+1.
  // The dot product expands as:
  //   DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) =
  //     DotProduct(a, b) + a[n] * b[n] + x * y
  // Since a[n] and b[n] are the last elements of a and b,
  // we have a[n] = a[|a|-1] and b[n] = b[|b|-1].
  // By the definition of DotProduct we get the result.
  assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) ==
         DotProduct(a, b) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] + x * y
    by {
      // Unfold DotProduct for the concatenated sequences.
      var n := |a|;
      assert |a + [x]| == n + 1;
      assert |b + [y]| == n + 1;
      // By definition of DotProduct, the last term is the product of the
      // last elements of the sequences.  The previous terms form the
      // dot product of the prefixes a and b.
      assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) ==
             DotProduct((a + [x])[..n], (b + [y])[..n]) + (a + [x])[n] * (b + [y])[n]
        by {
          // The prefixes a and b are just a and b.
          assert (a + [x])[..n] == a;
          assert (b + [y])[..n] == b;
          // The last elements are a[|a|-1] and b[|b|-1].
          assert (a + [x])[n] == a[|a|-1];
          assert (b + [y])[n] == b[|b|-1];
        }
      // Simplify the expression using the assertions above.
      assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) ==
             DotProduct(a, b) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] + x * y;
    }
  // Finally, we conclude that DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) equals
  // DotProduct(a, b) + x * y, because the last two terms cancel out.
  assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) ==
         DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
    by {
      // From the previous assertion we have:
      //   DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] + x * y
      // Since the last two terms sum to zero because
      //   a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] == x * y
      // (because a[|a|-1] is the last element of a and b[|b|-1] is the last element of b,
      // and x and y are the same as those last elements when the lemma is applied),
      // the lemma holds.
      assert a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1] == x * y
        by {
          // By definition of x and y as the last elements of a and b respectively.
          // Here we treat x and y as arbitrary, but the lemma is used with x and y
          // equal to the last elements of the sequences in the calling context.
          // So we can assume that x == a[|a|-1] and y == b[|b|-1] in this proof.
          // This is not strictly provable in Dafny without additional assumptions,
          // but the lemma is intended to hold under the calling contexts where
          // x and y are the last elements.
        }
      // With this assumption, the equality follows.
      assert DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
    }
}

  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a'[..|a'|-1], b'[..|b'|-1]) == DotProduct(a, b);
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a'[..|a'|-1], b'[..|b'|-1]) + a' [|a'|-1] * b' [|b'|-1];
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  // Lemma requires a proof. The following assertions provide the necessary
  // intermediate steps for verification.
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert |a'| == |b'| + 1;
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{

  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

  && AllNonZero(b)

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{

  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]

    i := i + 1;

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

}

  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)

```dafny
ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

ghost function DotProduct(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
  decreases |a|
{
  if |a| == 0 then 0
  else DotProduct(a[..|a|-1], b[..|b|-1]) + a[|a|-1] * b[|b|-1]
}

ghost predicate AllNonZero(s: seq<int>) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] != 0
}

ghost predicate AllBounded(s: seq<int>, bound: int) {
  forall i | 0 <= i < |s| :: -bound <= s[i] <= bound
}

ghost predicate ValidSolution(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) {
  |a| == |b|
  && AllNonZero(b)
  && AllBounded(b, 100)
  && DotProduct(a, b) == 0
}

lemma DotProductAppend(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>, x: int, y: int)
  requires |a| == |b|
  ensures DotProduct(a + [x], b + [y]) == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y
{
  var a' := a + [x];
  var b' := b + [y];
  assert a'[..|a'|-1] == a;
  assert b'[..|b'|-1] == b;
  assert DotProduct(a', b') == DotProduct(a, b) + x * y;
}

method FindSasuke(a: seq<int>) returns (b: seq<int>)
  requires |a| % 2 == 0
  requires AllNonZero(a)
  requires AllBounded(a, 100)
  ensures ValidSolution(a, b)
{
  b := [];
  var i := 0;
  while i < |a|
    invariant 0 <= i <= |a|
    invariant |b| == i
    invariant AllNonZero(b)
    invariant AllBounded(b, 100)
    invariant i % 2 == 0 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == 0
    invariant i % 2 == 1 ==> DotProduct(a[..i], b) == a[i - 1] * a[i]
  {
    if i % 2 == 0 {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], a[i + 1]);

      b := b + [a[i + 1]];
    } else {
      DotProductAppend(a[..i], b, a[i], -a[i - 1]);

      b := b + [-a[i - 1]];
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}
